  <span id="freeText17239748607459173505" style="display:none">DNF @ 70%<br /><br />I just can't. I'm calling it. I'm so over this book that I have been trying for months to plow through. I only pick it up between finishing a book and finding something else that I actually want to read, and at those times when I do pick this up, I skim so narrowly that I am hardly getting any story at all. <br /><br />The writing is very good, there's no doubt about that. <b>Perez-Reverte is a good author. However, the writing is so incredibly <i>dense</i> that if you aren't 100% invested in the fate of the character it is agonizing.</b> I hate Teresa Mendoza. She's obnoxious, whiny, holier-than-though, and straight-up vulgar. Some people love this kind of character, but I, 21-going-on-74 prudish cat-lady, absolutely do not. <br /><br />(Note: I only even attempted to read this because my mom liked the show and bought me the book. Sorry, Mom.) <br /><br /><br /><b>Popsugar 2020 Reading Challenge:</b> A book you meant to <s>read</s> finsih in 2019<br /><b>Around the Year in 52 Books Reading Challenge:</b> A book that is between 400-600 pages</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('qvzSklfPEuP78p+8NrD2hxYHOawDXx3EYQdZInqLsenlVn8OeVGpb27mYKwTVOf7ELPeemJjoMsYxTu0VvCdmg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

      <div id="aboutAuthor" class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/author/show/40398.Arturo_P_rez_Reverte">About Arturo PÃ©rez-Reverte</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class='bookAuthorProfile'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__topContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__photoContainer'>
<a href="/author/show/40398.Arturo_P_rez_Reverte"><div class='bookAuthorProfile__photo' style='background-image: url(https://images.gr-assets.com/authors/1415196332p3/40398.jpg);'></div>
</a></div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__widgetContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__name'>
<a href="/author/show/40398.Arturo_P_rez_Reverte">Arturo PÃ©rez-Reverte

followers

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer7928643576179027501">Spanish novelist and ex-journalist. He worked as a war reporter for twenty-one years (1973 - 1994). He started his journalistic career writing for the now-defunct newspaper <i>Pueblo</i>. Then, he jumped to news reporter for TVE, Spanish national channel. As a war journalist he traveled to several countries, covering many conflicts. He put this experience into his book 'Territorio Comanche', focusing on </span>
  <span id="freeText7928643576179027501" style="display:none">Spanish novelist and ex-journalist. He worked as a war reporter for twenty-one years (1973 - 1994). He started his journalistic career writing for the now-defunct newspaper <i>Pueblo</i>. Then, he jumped to news reporter for TVE, Spanish national channel. As a war journalist he traveled to several countries, covering many conflicts. He put this experience into his book 'Territorio Comanche', focusing on the years of Bosnian massacres. That was in 1994, but his debut as a fiction writer started in 1983, with 'El hÃºsar', a historical novella inspired in the Napoleonic era. <br /><br />Although his debut was not quite successful, in 1988, with 'The Fencing Master', he put his name as a serious writer of historic novels. That was confirmed in 1996, when was published the first book of his Captain Alatriste saga, which has been his trademark. After this book, he could leave definitely journalism for focusing on his career as a fiction writer. This saga, that happens in the years of the Spanish golden age, has seen, for now, seven volumes, where PÃ©rez-Reverte shows, from his particular point of view, historical events from Spanish history in the 16th century.<br /><br />Apart from these, he also penned another successful works like Dumas Club and Flanders Panel, titles that, among others, made PÃ©rez-Reverte one of the most famous and bestseller authors of Spanish fiction of our era.</span>
  <a data-text-id="7928643576179027501" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

</div>
</div>
